    <!-- My Script -->

    <!-- glidejs -->
    <script defer src="/static/js/glide.min.js"></script>
    <script defer>

        const glide_config = {
            type: 'carousel',
            perView: 6,
            perTouch: 2,
            breakpoints: {
                800: {
                    perView: 4,
                },
                600: {
                    perView: 3,
                },
                400: {
                    perView: 2,
                }
            }
        }

        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
            new Glide('.glide', glide_config).mount()
        })

        document.addEventListener('alpine:init', () => {
            Alpine.data('history', function () {
                return {
                    historyArr: [],
                    async init() {
                        let currentHistoryArr = await idbKeyval.get("history");
                        this.historyArr = (currentHistoryArr || []).map(history => ({
                            ...history,
                            series_name: this.decodeHTMLEntities(history.series_name)
                        }))
                    },
                    async clearHistory() {
                        await idbKeyval.del("history");
                        this.historyArr = []
                    },
                    decodeHTMLEntities(str) {
                        return str.replace(/&34;/g, '"').replace(/&39;/g, "'");
                    }
                };
            })
        });

    </script>
